1983 July 26 - Flagstaff Satsang

Adano83_07_26FlagstaffSatsangQ2NW3 - Many of us may not know too much of the meaning of Darshan and even those who are initiated sometimes have vague understanding of the word itself, the mechanics, let alone what is involved in the experience. Before we meditate the brain, before it entered the house, it’s in a state of excitement getting here, trying to decide for the traffic, it really can’t dip deep into the core of its structure. So at a Satsang which means fellowship with truth, the individual who is the focal point who has been spending many years dipping into this potential of their nature, acts of a sort of a resonating device that lines up the alpha wave of the brain of the student so that the brain can then dip into a non-verbal state. So you feel like for a brief moment everything is suspended, there are no words coming up, you’re in a state of expectancy but that state, that brief moment is known as Darshan, the whole sight, the devotion of heart, not of brain. There is no verbalization, the internal dialogue has temporarily suspended itself between left and right halves of the brain. Now it gives you the initiate and the word initiate simply means the individual who is going to work on their internal mechanism and has the privilege to work with it by being locked in to certain laws of nature and having prepared themselves by cleaning the body, making it less toxic, they can better resonate with their inner consciousness. In the olden days they would call that baptism and when Jesus went to John he said, “You baptize me” and John said, “No you baptized me” and picture two grown people arguing who should throw water on each other’s head. But then he said “Suffer it to be so for this is the way of righteousness” which merely means relate to the inner laws by synchronicity with someone who has delved deep in to synchronize. That doesn’t make the person superior to you or somebody pull you by the nose, it is like going to a battery charger and renovating the battery and bringing it back up to full charge so we do need these periodical encounters which is called Satsang. Now it can be in the presence of the person or in the absence of the person so we realize the form is not the connecting link, it’s the attitude. That’s why he said “suffer it to be so,” it other words go in, suspend the internal dialogue so that the potential that you are begins to come up. Those who have never been initiated they’ll also feel a charge that will stir them to want to know how to actually work in the detoxification and centering of themselves. It’s a sort of an encouragement to the individual and those who have already been initiated, it’s a reinforcement of what you call your annual carburetor tune-up, getting the machine to be more and more specific to its internal potential. So it has two advantages: one, it helps to suspend the internal dialogue that is so difficult to do being involved in living in this environment that is composed of sonics and you can’t help talking, from the day you’re born everybody’s talking to you. Even when you go to bed, you’re dreaming that someone’s talking inside so you do need periods to suspend that dialog just to get centering. I know you may have lots of questions and answers that you’re waiting for but before we take that as initiates, just to bring ourselves back to the important concept of our nature. One person asked “what is the most important role as a human being?” And this was the answer that came back from many many religious and spiritual leaders and even if you track it down historically in the writings, the importance is to realize you are an initiate of the highest consciousness, to realize that you have the tools to work with internally, scientifically to validate your true reality, and it has nothing to do with the individual or individuals who come and go, they are just the finished product. It’s up to you to finish your job and go through the process and realize it. We pay respect to those who go ahead of us, yes, because they’re the ones who innately sense their true potential either by sickness or some intense yearning from a previous life or because they have some function to perform while they’re alive but whatever drives them to that research, from that moment on you’re involved with a non-image, love for God. “Thou shalt have no other graven image before Me.” It is your contribution to the you in you to prove it once and for all that He became you and that’s why they instituted initiation or baptism thousands of years ago and it doesn’t matter what school or avenue we come from or use to get that, many roads lead to the door right here. It doesn’t matter how many roads it took to get here and I had to fly in an airplane to get here, yet I have to come through that one door, see what I mean? 0:10 The door is in the heart and that’s how Yogananda would say “Door of my heart open wide I keep for Thee. Wilt Thou come, wilt Thou come, just for once come to me.” “Even just once incarnation give me the living experience of my potential, restore my memory, restore my conviction of the reality that Creator has become his Creation. No longer lets me live in the conflicts or intra-polarity of the right brain and left brain. Let me center, let me have what they call peace that passes understanding.” It’s not a peace that the world gives, the world gives you six feet under the ground, it’s called tranquility in the grave and may you rest in peace. The peace of the initiate or the Soul Potential is the strength of peace, the capacity to keep coping with daily challenges and going through them. This peace the world can’t give us, only the Christ nature in you, the God nature in you gives you that from your self-confrontation but you need human beings to divert your attention to that point of reference. They may be called teachers or guides or Gurus, what is more important, not they, is that the student is not greater than the teacher and the teacher not greater than the student, they both got to go there. We both have to come to this door to greet each other tonight so our roles are not important, who is teacher and who is student, what is important we are initiates of the Spirit. We are initiated into the Spirit to find our own potential, we are baptized, we are brought into the inner contact devoid of outer trappings, devoid of outer images. We start off our early growth by relating to images and finally we mature into the one real temple because Creative Life lives in it. One of the hardest things in this process is to know another human being can hurt you after you’ve done things for them, what would generate compassion from your heart for them? Yet a parent has to generate compassion for his child regardless if the child does all kinds of things. So you’re given preparation in compassionate love from the time you become a parent, let alone humanity. That is the basis of the growth of your spirituality, that’s what we’re looking for. It’s a non-verbal relationship, more and more it’s the internal joyousness to release it but even teachers get angry and tear down the money changers you know and drive them out of the church saying “You’re making it a gambling place.” They’ll spank us once in a while or pull our ears and let us know “quit your nonsense” once in a while, get on the ball and look in at yourself, that comes occasionally. So sometimes there are a lot of dry periods in your spiritual process when you feel that you’re left out but you’re not. As soon as the internal dialogue suspends itself, it’s flashing up again, the realization goes up. And that’s why the institution or the idea came of “when two or three are gathered in My name, there am I in the midst.” This is more intended scientifically for the initiate than for the regular person who is just interested in meeting in a meditation meeting because the real communication goes on with the initiate from that standpoint with his own Christ nature. He is pulling together his Christ nature and allowing it to release its potential through this mechanism. That’s why “when two or three are gathered in My name,” not in me Jesus or me Adano, it’s when we as initiates gather into the sense of remembrance at the time of initiation, that contact it pulls and nurtures and feeds and a Darshan, or whole sight, total sight, that is the capacity to see through, not see at. It’s a feeling that you sense when it’s occurring like a suspension, that is the whole name, “in My name.” The Creative Intelligence is Sonics and we can call Him God or Father, some people call Him all types of names. American Indians call Him Great Spirit but it’s a vibrancy that is exchanged at the human level, that makes it more important as an experience than something that has happening and there are no human beings around. It is when you meet another human being and that human being is locking into the potential and can allow this vibrancy to emanate, then you in turn, it’s like a magnet, you become magnetized, you can now release it yourself, it works through you also. My experience came from my teacher and I give the credit to him and he will always say his came from his teacher and we all go back and say “Okay God, You did Your thing” but that’s fine and good, we respect that. The important thing is that you know it works and you know it exists and it’s not a verbal experience, it’s a non-verbal experience of presence. Meditation is the nurturing and trying to always retain the feeling of the Darshan or the effect or the sensation that occurred during initiation. Meditation is that particular nurturing attitude to recapture it or to re-enhance it and the more you meditate, the more you’ll re-enhance it to the extent where it starts bubbling inside of you. Put it this way, my good friend the Pentecostal minister says “You don’t need no alcohol from the bottle, I got enough alcohol going inside of me, it bubbles into champagne” and that’s what this sensation of the whole Spirit the whole sight is all about is that same principle. 0:20 This sensitivity of knowing that it’s waves that suspend the verbal dialogue and allow you to feel and reach out to the memory banks of various levels of yourself. Now I know when you take a little drink you always feel like like you’re “out there?” Good. As my friend would say, “this is a natural high,” but that’s exactly what you’re trying to enhance. The main goal behind that or process behind that more than a goal is a cellular transformation is occurring in you though you may not realize it at the time. As an initiate as you become more conscious and meditate, that means enhancing and trying to re-enhance that feeling and having the verbal dialogue suspending itself more and more, an immunity begins to increase. You can cut yourself it heals very fast, you can seem to deprive yourself of many things you couldn’t do before and a gradual strength and self-confidence, a strength of peace to cope with conditions of life becomes obvious, you’re getting stronger in yourself. You realize that and you’re no longer running to find the happiness in secluded areas, you’re standing on your two feet and experiencing the happiness and the peace of mind right where you are. You start out searching and running to different areas for the peace, only to return back to find it’s already bubbling up. That is to say in the early stages of your encounter with Spirit you’re like the grape on the vine, then initiation is like somebody plucked you off the vine and they did this to you, (laughter) and your dry spells has got to do with all this stuff here. Periodically they’ll put this in the jar and it starts the fermentation, it’s gonna be very tricky job too because it can be wine or vinegar, but we can’t stop at the wine because that would be a psychic level of our growth. It’s good, don’t get me wrong, that is called gift of Spirit but it’s not fruit of Spirit. It is the next stage, the enhancing where Satsang is. You meet the person or they’re not even there, the Satsang doesn’t stop, the Satsang is going on now at a cellular level inside with eyes open or eyes shut. The verbal dialogue can be suspended now at your command, this is shifting into the champagne level. Therefore they call that Samadhi or God-realization in the waking state, the moving state, that’s the champagne state. Wine is the non-moving state where you sit down like this and you’re drunk with it but the moment you get up, it’s all gone, you rush back, that’s the wine state. So you’re afraid to get up and move around lest the verbalizations keep rushing back in and the peace seems to get weaker but don’t quit, just go again. And it’s being reinforced by those who love you as in the Eye of the Cyclone written by Dr. Lilly, you’re not without others looking on who are deeply concerned with your well-being no matter what level you’re at, that’s nice to know. But no matter what level you think you’re in, there’s always somebody watching to pull you back up and that’s good to know that we never really can fall short of the Creative Presence. So out of sight is not out of mind, you’re always in tune with the individual and it pulls you up so you can move from the wine stage or the non-moving stage to the champagne stage, the ever-moving stage, that’s the purpose behind it to get you there to be your own bottle of champagne and flip out your own cork (laughter). And Darshan or Satsang is that intent, that’s the whole intent behind it, the whole mechanics behind it is to get you the initiated grape to move on into the champagne level of yourself. That’s the students went to Jesus and he said “If I don’t touch your feet, you’re not in me.” If I don’t make contact with you or if you don’t see or relate or get together, there is no enhancing of (inaudible). See that’s how for centuries Man realized that a Satsang or a group sitting down was more important than books. Books are good but books don’t give you the level of non-verbalization, you have to sit down in the presence with loved ones and activate the memory that triggered you in the first place to be interested in yourself and feel that vibrancy permeate you and suspend the verbalization and that allows you to extend that nonverbal quality longer and longer to the extent that you can get up and walk with it. Another quality of Satsang, which is fellowship or two or three gatherings in my Name, is the exposure to transfiguration. When the disciples were with their teacher Jesus in the Garden and he asked them to pray a while with him which means to sit down and suspend the verbalization, later on one said that they saw two other great Souls standing next to the teacher: Moses and Elijah and one brave soul said, Peter, “we’ll make a tabernacle or a covenant,” we’ll make a commitment at this point in time in our own nature to really try to suspend the verbalization so that we can have more of this exposure to the transfiguration. Transfiguration is both visual and internal, biological. You may see facial changes on the person, interposing phases of the unity of the atom and the oneness of life at the visual level. That’s just the skin of the banana, the real banana you want to eat now let alone get the oil, comes from inside. The real eternal transfiguration is the closing of the eyes and at the portal door where all of us merge, we come through embracing you from inside then you are transfigured. 0:30 And they have only one message for you, “We who have crossed the threshold of silence yearn for you to cross that threshold and to merge in the unity of yourself and may you be transfigured into your eternal Now. Then a strange thing will happen, when you open the eyes to look out you may not see anything for a few seconds and you’ll wonder where you are, don’t get scared. Having crossed the threshold of silence, you’ve crossed the threshold of Sonics which means the Father outside of the vibratory creation. The Father as a Son, He’s His own Son, is the Creative Intelligence in the vibratory creation of sonics, “You see me, you see the Father but I go unto the Father,” that came later. The realized Man goes on to the next level, he has to go on to the next level but he must experience the first level of hearing the Sonics, having an outward exposure to the transfiguring experience of physical laws, things seem to go hazy, it’s like looking down the road on a hot day. Don’t get scared, it’s just natural laws going on, you’re not hallucinating and it’s occurring naturally within you, it’s allowing you to have total sight into the reality. Then you’ll cross that threshold where there is no verbalization, there is no matching, there is no language in it. For that brief moment you have crossed through there, you are with the Father then you know for sure without doubt, He became (inaudible). Ego, individuality are all left behind in the Sonic level, in the verbalization level and a collective unity of oneness is very very pronounced in your mechanism. So I can appreciate your feeling when you said “you’re afraid you’re gonna (inaudible)” that was because you were feeling it at a sonic level in the engulfment with the water because in a strange way you survived, that intimacy of compassion plucked you to the next level and from now on you can cross the threshold and go into your Divinity. Do not be afraid of your divinity and you may admit like Saint Catherine, “Give me back my brother Jesus” because she sees her own self, she prefers to have someone to respect, we all do that. I myself looks to Yogananda or living teachers because one cannot really worship a total non-image even though it became you. It would be a sense of non-appreciation for those who went before you who made you conscious but whatever time they triggered that consciousness in you to recognize it. So you are no longer afraid or feel threatened by paying respect or loving adoration to the person who triggered you. That’s how they wrote the book later on “At the Feet of the Master” but you don’t see his face, you just see the foot and many Gurus have the name “foot of God.” A lot of these highly realized Masters, when you translate their name it’s called paw or foot of God or the toe of God and it’s very interesting the names that they have. It’s no discredit to any of us, it’s so fantastically loving, you just love it. Everyone is. If you feel to close your eyes and merge do so, if you feel to keep your eyes open do so, let presence flow. Fill yourself with presence, let your potential come to the surface, you’re aiming for champagne. (Gap in tape). Audience: I want to hear your exposition on the enlightenment of the unmarried person, the everyday person. Adano: We use the word enlightenment but sometimes we really don’t connect the experience, what it represents in terms of the spiritual life. In the spiritual life the enlightenment is the ability to recognize moment to moment the intrinsic timing of events occurring around you. How you as an individual is at a certain location, a certain time, and your reaction to the conditions based upon your expectancy. In the olden days they would say every action is determined by God, His will be done, but we never really can cope with it or get any experience to say that it’s God’s will and if we fail we do say it’s His will and if we win we do say it’s His will but we never really understand what is His will in the first place in terms of the practical exposure, practical day-to-day living. So we tend to search for enlightenment as if it is going to totally eradicate all the veils of the existence. The enlightenment in the daily life and for the human being more than the ordinary man or woman, the human being per say, in the true spiritualness is recognition of timing. Many of you drove a lot of vehicles to come here, right? Did you buy sixty five hundred dollars worth of parts or sixty five hundred dollars worth of timing? Yet in a simple rational practical existence, it’s taken for granted until it’s brought into focus what you really have and what you’re really experiencing and what frees you now from guilt complex. Spirituality aims to free you from guilt in the experience and aims to let you have the enlightenment or the understanding to be correct that doesn’t have a feedback of guilt because there is no good or bad. 0:40 Like Omar Khayyam would say “I myself am heaven and hell” but heaven in the sense of a haven or reservoir, hell in the sense of “h-e-l-d,” I’m held back by my own inability to time myself. Nobody is holding me back, I am holding my one-self back and that is because I’m out of time and if we look at production and production simply represents repetition, you can say “rosary” now, mechanical rosary, repeating over and over, Xeroxing, do you see? You’re getting the understanding, you’re getting the enlightenment then you’re again recognizing that you’re forced to synchronize with timing. That automatically liberates you from a guilt process of living that drains you off and then you feel left out and in actuality it’s not true. The enlightenment or the freedom from, that’s why he said “free men all, lord of yourself” but s-e-l-f can be very misleading and can be very nebulous and very authoritative and very deistic whereas c-e-l-l, “free men all, lord of the cell,” lord of these cells. This is an intrinsic battery, each one of them, it’s an intrinsic machinery, it’s an intrinsic powerhouse, it’s a conditioned atom. You as consciousness is in-resident in it and the interconnectedness of timing makes you more appreciative of it therefore freeing you of the guilt feedbacks as you become synchronized to its internal rhythms. The whole frontier of reality opens itself for you now in the unlimitedness of it that there is no limitation to God, it is called to the greater glory of God. To this end Jesus healed the blind man, not because of karma if he from a past life that he is born blind or the parents which is heredity but it’s the challenge within each one of us to pull it together in the cellular structure and realize or feel and time yourself, lock into your intrinsic timing now recognized as the true will of God. Why would the Creator create to punish? He doesn’t punish, He provides one basic law for the whole creation to function on, we know as Newton’s first law, right? In the East we know it as karma and to the churchianistic thinking it is “what you sow, you reap,” and the cowboys are singing it now, (inaudible) but karma or whatever you want to call it is still centered on timing. If you look at it objectively and don’t be swayed by its forcefulness on you, you will free the brain from the feedback of guilt and look at it as the opportunity to rise above your limitations and that is really the full enlightenment of the human being. “To him that overcometh,” I will do what? “I wouldn’t send forth a second time.” You see all these things are coming to have more valid meaning and possible experience. Before it would seem nebulous not when you look at it in terms of timing and when you have to live a day-to-day life of basic survival regardless of what you believe in and when the cost factor of existence tells you where it’s at, put up or shut up, then you know timing is God’s will in your life like it or not. It doesn’t take away from the old traditional way of describing the sacredness of God to you, in fact it removes the weakness of it with your own self-fear of integrating with it and it imparts a strength which you never had before and that’s the strength of peace. “The peace I give, the world don’t give,” the peace that comes from within your own I AM-ness of understanding your structure. This is strength, you can live it and not feel threatened by it and to sum it up in a working behavior of enlightenment or understanding, it is acting what you say to yourself. Years ago when I came into this area and I happened to go on the reservation and I grew up hearing this statement many times when they said that the Indians accused the white man of speaking with a forked tongue and I always wanted to know what that really meant and I have a friend who I’m going to see pretty soon and he said “pale face speak with forked tongue.” And I looked at my tongue in the mirror and I couldn’t see where it was forked and then try to get their version, “he lies, he doesn’t convey what he means” but that’s not really what it was. The Indian on the reservation today or in the frontier days realized that in their structural language, it was designed to act what they say. Whereas in english it’s not so designed, one word has many different meanings and this creates a conflict when spoken to another person who is linearly conditioned to act out what he says and doesn’t have flexibility. Then he will accuse you for being double talking and meaning different shades of the meaning and therefore you can get into all kind of wrong understandings in communication. Yet by the same token, rigid language, linear in itself can be a prison and a flexible language can be a treasure. You can restrict yourself in one word with one meaning and at the same time you can liberate yourself with that same word by having a different meaning especially if you’re traumatized, I’ll give you an example. For the actual layman, as you would say, looking for enlightenment moment to moment, d-o-g, now you must be thankful to english the only language you can do this with, d-o-g is man’s best friend, agreed? You spell it backwards it’s still the man’s best friend. (Laughter). 0:50 Now you can’t do that with any other language no matter how you try so we have a unique experience here by speaking english. Many nationalities can use for the first time a guilt-free communication to their internal self, it’s very very interesting because you don’t feel threatened no more as you begin to look at the simplicity and the naturalness of the language and the timing of the events. Years ago, I’ll give you an example in my own life, I’d an appointment to go to and I’d always think I would be late so I’m in a hurry to get there before and I’d get worked up with the feeling “I’m late, I don’t want to get late.” So you burn up so much energy worrying about being late by the time you get there, all the red lights are in your favor. (Laughter). So one day I said to myself, “enough of this wanting to be late, why can’t the other guy be late and I be early? Why should I think that I’m going to be late, can he not be late?” I reversed the mental attitude, not feeling guilt or wishing him any kind of a bad accident or anything and so for the first time when I saw it work, I laughed, I arrived at my destination all green lights and he’s busy apologizing for the red lights. (Laughter). Audience: I understand the timing with regards to outside events but how can we become conscious of the timing of our own selves? Adano: Time is a word that will make a lot of us think it does not exist since it’s being conscious of where you are and you have to use your cells by breathing to be self-conscious and therefore you could say to yourself you have all the time in the world because all time is really Now and there is really no yesterday and there is really no tomorrow. Whatever occurred yesterday occurred in the Now of yesterday. Whatever will occur tomorrow will be in the Now of tomorrow when it occurs. So we can go around in circles talking to ourselves from within but eventually you will find that you will verbally zero in on the internal atomic light of the cell and then you would have a true picture of timing in the cellular structure. The distance light crosses the width of an electron is a unit of time in the cell. You are an atom conditioned onto a cellular form, you carry a tremendous power within you, the capacity to monitor called consciousness. Yet the only way you can validate it is to look inward and that’s the direction every teacher gives, “When the eyes,” not one, he said both, “are single,” now how could you make two eyes single? Try as you like, looking outside it could never be single, it would be distorting all around. The only way it could singularly focus or singularly refer itself to or center itself, you have to close then you have a single vision and then closed vision. “When the eyes are single, the whole body,” now this is more scientific now, it’s getting more scientific, no reference to any object outside the whole body, the whole cellular mechanism, “IS,” not was, IS “full,” capacity, “of light.” Now imagine a cellular mechanism being monitored by its own cell capabilities, the maximum light potential locked up in it and to zero in on specific measurements, each cell, each unit would involve light. And therefore a unit of time, if you’re going to say time means an emission of this, that’s time spelled backward, “e-m-i-t,” because this is really an emission mechanism and what is an emission, it’s an energy field. As we get more specific, more objective and intrinsic, it has to go across certain dimensions and so to put it in a unit measurement to make it repetitious to be practical to survive, we will eventually recognize that this timing is propelling itself from within the atomic structure and therefore the distance it will travel across the width of the electron would give you your unit of timing inside of you. “The light is shining in the darkness,” here you become trapped now for the first time because when you look inside you see darkness and yet if you remember when you were initiated you saw a light within you, right? “And the light is shining in the darkness but the darkness comprehends it not,” the very cell that is circular, that contains light, sets of a force field of darkness to compress the light, keeping the light in a state of “capsuled down.” The more you verbalize, the more the light disappears because you’re putting up a shield in front of it. The less you’ve verbalize, which is called the internal dialogue, the less you want to match words or your programming from the environment, the more the light seems to expand. “Let your light so shine,” that means diminish the verbalization in order for the force field of light to fill out and take over and push away the darkness. Before who? “Let your light so shine before who?” It only says Man, your fellow Man. “That they may see the good works and glorify the Father which is in you.” Others will feel or sense or actually see by the eyes when it’s open this glow of total vision and they will sense a synchronicity with you. 1:00 From that moment on, whatever you put in the brain as a program like a computer, it punches up. Now picture for one moment you’re in the place of the mind of Jesus, as Paul says “Give me that mind that was in Christ” and you’re sitting there and somebody says to you “Lazarus is dead” and if you don’t have any comprehension of what you are intrinsically, you may not be able to say “Lazarus come forth.” Now imagine when you said “Lazarus come forth,” out of the grave says “No boss, I ain’t getting up for you.” That blows away all your realization about yourself but if the mechanism of Lazarus gets up and comes out and then you the person who is applying the law would suddenly say “Father, I didn’t have to say it in a loud voice, only because of the people around.” Light, sonics, timing, rhythm. Now this phenomenon is not restricted only to the man Jesus because he was the very first man to say “The things I do, you will do also and greater things shall you do.” That lays the groundwork for greater things for him to experience too but if he says “Not greater than me” and “no further than this,” then you know where you are and you know who he is. But the principle doesn’t do that in the mechanism, the principle is giving you greater and greater possibilities of yourself which then makes you more conscious of the internal cellular timing to the demand and you can’t express it before the demand is there. You couldn’t command the force to move if there is no demand. Who would fill a full cup, you see what I mean? So you couldn’t express any motion on your part if there is no demand for it, the timing is always evidence of the demand and your ability to synchronize to fit the demand. So again no-thing moves except by Divine Will, there is no object moving in proper synchronicity if it wants to perform efficiently. If it doesn’t want to perform efficiently it would be out of what? Synchronicity. Everything to perform efficiently must be in its state of synchronicity, this is Divine Will, nothing moves except by Divine Will. It’s another way of saying no physical function or cosmic function or intrinsic function is occurring without synchronicity. So don’t feel that timing, though reduced to represent Divine Will, is a mundane thing, it’s not a mundane thing, it’s a very sacred thing so sacred that you don’t violate or try to push it. You know what they say “You don’t break a law of nature, you break yourself against it” and that’s how we learn the hard way. It that clear enough? Audience: So guessing that timing that is proper is more or less anticipating the events that are going to happen? Adano: I’ll have to quote Sri Yukteswar, “God is un-anticipatory, ever-new joy” and though we may foretell our future conditions, it doesn’t compel us to experience it. Therefore the stars may foretell but they don’t compel and by this we learn now the deeper impact of timing on our lives, we have a freedom in timing. We don’t exercise it because we don’t know how to exercise it and the only time we can exercise this freedom is in a necessity. That’s why the scriptural writings that the Eastern teachers would say “All your needs are fulfilled,” they didn’t say all your wants are fulfilled. So life as a functional process is a necessity motivated synchronous organism comprising your cellular structure as the ultimate form of experience, do you get it now? I’ll cook your food in a clean pot, plate, and everything, everything will be meticulous, and nothing will have anything to do with mine” and that was the agreement “Don’t make me into you.” It’s like saying “daisy don’t convert me into a rose.” All right, this went on for many years and they lived happily together and one day the teacher came for a visit to this country and he invites the teacher to their home and he told the teacher what a great wife he has, that she would cook food for him without any meat or anything. The teacher said all right and they went to the house and it was lunchtime and they got to the table and there was the wife, cooked the food and their food was separate food and the teacher looked at her straight like that and as he sat down he says, “I’ll initiate you.” Now that blew this man’s whole entire mind, here he for years been… and when he went to India he had to clean up his act and clean up his body before he could get initiated, be a vegetarian to some extent, and here she’s been eating and nipping, puffing, and she’s gonna be initiated right away. Her devotion is a devotion of the heart.” But he didn’t say a devotion to what, it left the man to figure out what the teacher meant. “Your devotion is a devotion of the brain. Whereas my wife simply cooked the food and you’re my husband and that’s all there is to it.” (Inaudible), she’s not going to offend her husband, he wants to eat no meat and don’t drink no alcohol and no smoke so she just did it and that was doing it from her heart as a wife. When Reverend Ley first came to the United States, he went to New York where he made his living working for a corporation. For those of you who are not familiar with the term Yoga, I might give you the definition from Webster’s dictionary which says “it is a practice involving intense and complete concentration on something, especially the Deity, in order to establish the identity of consciousness with the object of concentration.” Usually it involves some certain postures and breathing is very important. So Reverend Ley taught Yoga and meditation classes for several years under the guidance of Paramahansa Yogananda. In 1969, while attending an East/West conference at Southern Methodist University in Dallas, Reverend Ley met Swami Anand Saraswati of New Delhi India who had been one of Mahatma Gandhi’s close aides in the movement for India’s independence. The Saraswati is an ancient Yogic order and its name indicates a spiritual path through knowledge and wisdom. Adano Ley was initiated into the Saraswati order and given the title of Swami Nityananda and again for those of you who are not too familiar with the term “Swami” is a Hindu title of respect for a religious teacher. In Western religion we just say Reverend. Reverend Ley had spent five years in solitary yogic retreat in California before receiving this honor and while continuing his work and teaching in Yoga and metaphysics, as well as lecturing around the country, Reverend Ley also acquired an ND degree and is a licensed Naturopathic physician. Sometimes you can feel the presence walk the room or you can feel the heightening of your senses but above all the peace that gives you strength to go on day-to-day moment-to-moment becomes self-evident. Some of us may see the form of some exalted Saint or Holy One, others may feel or hear the internal music but that is not the full measure of the spiritual intent. The full measure of the special intent is to be able to open your eyes and function here consciously with that internal strength increasing in you. 1984 July 26 - Sedona Sermon on the Mount

Adano84_07_26SedonaSermonontheMountQ2NW1 - Audience: This is indeed a very auspicious occasion for Jeanette and myself. Most of you, certainly many of you know of Adano and his background. I know him as a very gentle, very humble, very beautiful person, and it’s our honor, Jeanette and I, to have you in our home tonight, to have you with us. Adano, the evening is yours. Adano: Thank you everyone and my wonderful hosts and Margaret for getting me here. Most of us have been exposed to what Jesus taught at the Sermon on the Mount but there are other things concerning that sermon which the average person is not aware of and even those who wrote it and recorded it did not infer too much. There is a relationship going on between the multitude, the student, and the teacher. The intimate exchange of spiritual ideas between the teacher and the student is not recognized or experienced by the multitude. That is why this particular process exists, a sort of a teacher/student relationship. The general public cannot be exposed to a direct psychophysical transformation on certain spiritual experiences but between the teacher and the student, that psychophysical exchange occurs every instant. In a group meeting like this, what we call Satsang or “When two or three are gathered in my name, there am I in the midst,” many of us don’t even know the extent of that statement, what is actually occurring. It takes many years to uncover that intimate exchange between a realized person and the student. The Sermon on the Mount was not just given for the public, it was given primarily for those 12 men who lived with Jesus and how to break their internal frustrations in their meditational process and how to arrive at an inward accomplishment in a very deep intimate psychophysical exchange, a transformation of their body, an actual bodily transformation for those men. It’s more than just a sermon on top of a mountain. To the average person, it sounds like a sermon on the mountain but to a the student on the path of truth, it’s his encounter with God in the realized man that opens avenues of power locked up in the student. For instance if a student is suffering with frustration from being hurt by people who pick on him but they can’t release it, how is the teacher going to break through that pattern and heal that person to open that they will become a channel for that teacher? He may give a counsel, some type of a statement that a student can relate to, that the general public can also relate to but would it help the general public? The student is the person that the teacher is more concerned with because he is the one that’s going to have to carry on when the teacher is gone in that process of self understanding, the process of self transformation. The general public will come and go so in the Eastern countries they say a teacher is like an elephant, he has a pair of tusks that keeps away the public from attacking him and his teeth is what he chews food with and that’s what the organs are fed with and that’s the disciple. His actual body is his disciple where he chews his food and nurtures it but the tusks keep everybody away from hurting him. The general public is not a disciple in the presence of realized people, only the intimacy that occurs with those who are ready for the path that has an interconnectedness and that’s why this type of tradition goes on, it will not stop. When Jesus was asked the way of truth he said, “None come unto the Father but by me.” The general public didn’t understand what he was talking about “but suffer it to be so for this is the way of righteousness.” It is the transformation that occurs between the realized person and the unrealized person as a bond which they call teacher/disciple relationship and when the two have arrived at that transformation, there is no teacher/disciple, it’s enough that they are friends because they’ve both broken the internal conflicts that separates them from the unified process of Beingness but the general public can’t experience that. 0:40 So until we realize what the Sermon on the Mount is involved with, we may go off in tangents trying to interpret the meanings of what he said. But then we look at it from the level of a disciple and a teacher relationship and not as a someone giving a sermon on a pulpit or a mountain top for the general public, we’re gonna experience something entirely different, far more intimate with the Creative Process and with the God-nature locked up in ourselves. You wouldn’t know if you’re going right or wrong. And especially when one is trying to realize his God-nature, it’s not an easy thing to realize. You may ask, how do you see a person? The answer is the eye. The eye is constructed like a camera. It has a dark chamber, a lens through which light is admitted, and a sensitive plate through which the light acts. In the human eye, the sensitive plate is the retina. Light acting on photo sensitive chemical substances in the retina creating impulses that are transmitted to the brain which interprets them as visual images. When you hear a sound, it too is converted into touch. You not only hear, but you feel it also as vibratory sensation. Similarly, light does not go into the brain as light, but acts on the photosensitive cells of the retina. The result is a chemical stimuli activating nerve impulses that travel to the brain and are converted there into mental images having form, line, and color. The retina is actually a thin out pocketing of the brain around which the eye has formed. In fact, when you see a person, you are not seeing him, but a photographic image. The power of vision is in the brain, but if the brain is anesthetized, you cannot see anything. Even when you become absent minded, your brain does not respond to the impulses coming into it from the retina. You are unaware of outer happenings. He will first come to you as a small image and as your power becomes stronger, it takes on the full form. 20 When you open your eyes fully, the vision will vanish. You will have to try harder to see him when the eyes are open. These experiences are tremendous, but can be only achieved with your deepest desire and love. So meditate until you make contact. The blessings of the guru and the grace of god is with us tonight. If you don’t see Christ right away, you will feel him. 25 I have been telling you this whole evening about Jesus and how to contact Him, but what is more important is the object of communion with the Christ Consciousness. For centuries, from Jerusalem to India, this earth plane has been hallowed by great souls who have all brought the same one message to us, that is the message of Self Realization, the Christ Intelligence which manifests throughout vibratory creation. A person cannot know of Jesus merely by reading a book on theology, scriptures, he must feel the presence of Jesus in deep meditation, he must have an experience of Christ Consciousness throughout vibratory creation. We must learn to seek this spiritual solace in the inner, immortal temple. 27 Let us enlarge the cup of our consciousness so that the Christ Consciousness can fill us and quench our Soul thirst. As we behold the Christ Consciousness in all individuals, families, races, creatures, we must finally experience Him in the spinal Christmas tree of the bodily temple. There we will discover the Star of Wisdom, the omnipresent Ever New Joy, the Cosmic Sound, Cosmic Light, Cosmic Vibration, Cosmic Wisdom, and Cosmic Love. Every year and every moment, the Christ is recognized in Cosmic Consciousness and the angelic beings all celebrate this glorious manifestation. Let us now celebrate this Christ Consciousness in our own meditation. Let us prepare the Christmas tree of the spine and let us place the eternal gifts on this beautiful spinal tree. The gift of eternal consciousness life, unconditional love, unattachment, service, understanding, self control, and self surrender. And as we place these gifts on the spinal column of the great cosmic Christmas tree, we behold the Cosmic Christ Consciousness permeating us in a golden, blue white light, flowing through us and around us and may this Consciousness lift us up that we be living examples of these glorious gifts and as we permeate our consciousness, not the physical body of Jesus, but the glorious Christ Consciousness that is in all creation, we will then participate of these glorious gifts that we feel in the spinal Christmas tree in the bodily temple. Om, Christ, Gurus. 30 Oh beloved Jesus, I surrender my ego to thy consciousness. May thy blessing flow through me to all these holy ones. As I touch them on their forehead, my thy blessing flow to them, granting them permanent Christ Consciousness in this bodily temple. And may they feel thy presence and behold the many masters who have made us conscious of thy presence. And may we live in this glorious consciousness and participate with this blessing. We thank thee. Om, Christ, Gurus. Adano stops for a moment, gap in tape. 37 Somebody else talking 40 Adano tells the story of Yogananda’s life. Babaji, the Supreme Master and Avatar made this statement years before Yogananda was born. “I see that you are interested in the West as well as the East.” “East and West must establish a golden middle path of activity and spirituality combined. We have much to learn from the West in material development and much to give in universal methods to the West in order for them to base their religious beliefs. You Swamaji have a part to play in the coming harmonious exchange between the East and the West. Some years hence I will send you a disciple whom you can train for Yoga dissemination in the West. The vibrations where of many spiritually seeking souls come flood like to me. I perceive potential saints in America and Europe waiting to be awakened.” You see Master’s life was preicted way before in a conversation between Supreme Master Babaji and Sri Yukteswar. Story about Yogananda praying for approval to go the West. Babaji came and gave him approval. This is all in Autobiography of a Yogi. gap in tape then somebody else talking. 50 Still somebody else talking. 60 Adano talking again. Beloved Master, perceive this great Cosmic Experience by gazing on the Supreme Master Babaji. Now, Master himself craved this experience to be a permanent thing within himself. Sri Yukteswar bestowed the divine experience of Cosmic Consciousness. The divine experience does not come by intellectual willingness or open mindedness. It descends through the enlargement of the consciousness and by devotion and through the natural inevitability of a divine nature, the student pulls at god with irresistible force and the cosmic vision is then drawn down within the seekers range of consciousness. As we close our eyes and gaze at the point between the eyebrows at the Christ center, slowly expanding our consciousness and beholding the golden light, the blue, the cosmic white star radiating, feeling our presence, traveling through our entire bodies into our rooms, the four walls. Beyond the four walls expanding to the very boundaries of our community, to the boundaries of our countries, and to the boundaries of other countries, expanding throughout the entire earth. Our consciousness is expanding to other planets, stars, galaxies, the entire creation. As we behold this cosmic chalice, this cosmic holy grail being filled with the divine spirit, the divine nature. Notes: Adano00_SolarAtHoustonClinicQ1 is probably April 1, 1989.

The Cherokee word for soul is ada:n(v)do. Its semantic meaning, deconstructed from its root, ada nv a, indicates that someone or something is in transit, moving from place to place. This transitory vision of this mutable and mobile essence has its origins, according to Fogelson, in the aboriginal Cherokee belief that four primal animate life forces emanate from the human body. From The Night Has a Naked Soul, by Alan Kilpatrick
